\"\"\"\n   161→        print(f\"Evolving population (input_dim={X_train.shape[1]})...\", flush=True)\n   162→\n   163→        pop = Population(\n   164→            population_size=ModelConfig.POPULATION_SIZE,\n   165→            model_types=ModelConfig.MODEL_TYPES,\n   166→            mutation_rate=ModelConfig.MUTATION_RATE,\n   167→ # Evaluate all individuals\n   177→            for i, ind in enumerate(pop.individuals):\n   178→                try:\n   179→                    print(f\"    Training individual                    pred = ind.model.predict(X_train, threshold=0.5)\n   183→                    accuracy = (pred == y_train).mean()\n   184→\n   185→                    # Simple fitness based on training accuracy (we'll validate on walk-forward later)\n   186→                    ind.fitness = accuracy\n   187→                    print(f\"      -> fitness={ind.fitness:.4f}\", flush=True)\n   188→                except Exception as e:\n   189→                    print(f\"      -> training error: {e}\", flush=True)\n   190→                    ind.fitness = -1000.0\n   191→\n   192→            # Evolve to next generation, but not after the final generation\n   193→            if gen < generations - 1:\n   194→                print(\"  Evolving to next generation...\", flush=True)\n   195→                pop.evolve()\n   196→\n   197→            best = pop.get_best(1)[0]\n   198→            print(f\"    Best fitness: {best.fitness:.4f} (model={best.model_type})\", flush=True)\n   199→\n   200→        return pop\n   201→\n   202→    def run_walk_forward(\n   203→        self,\n   204→        df: pd.DataFrame\n   205→    ) -> Dict[str, float]:\n   206→        \"\"\"\n   207→        Run walk-forward validation with a single temporal split.\n   208→        Train on data before the validation period, test on the most recent validation period.\n   209→        This provides an honest OOS performance estimate without leakage.\n   210→        \"\"\"\n   211→        print(\"Running walk-forward validation (single split)...\", flush=True)\n   212→\n   213→        df_sorted = df.sort_values(\"open_time\").reset_index(drop=True)\n   214→\n   215→        # Determine validation period length (e.g., 7 days)\n   216→        val_days = ValidationConfig.VALID_DAYS\n   217→        val_rows = int(val_days * 24 * 60 / 15)  # number of 15-min candles\n   218→\n   219→        total_rows = len(df_sorted)\n   220→        if total_rows < val_rows + 1000:\n   221→            print(\"Insufficient data for walk-forward split.\", flush=True)\n   222→            return {\"accuracy\": 0.0, \"bets_per_month\": 0.0, \"n_folds\": 0}\n   223→\n   224→        # Split: validation = most recent val_rows, training = older data\n   225→        valid_df = df_sorted.iloc[-val_rows:].copy()\n   226→        train_df = df_sorted.iloc[:-val_rows].copy()\n   227→\n   228→        # Limit training samples to most recent MAX_TRAIN_SAMPLES (controls memory/time)\n   229→        if len(train_df) > ModelConfig.MAX_TRAIN_SAMPLES:\n   230→            train_df = train_df.tail(ModelConfig.MAX_TRAIN_SAMPLES).copy()\n   231→            print(f\"Limited training to {len(train_df)} most recent samples\", flush=True)\n   232→\n   233→        print(f\"Train: {len(train_df)} samples, Validation: {len(valid_df)} samples\", flush=True)\n   234→\n   235→        X_train = train_df[self.feature_names]\n   236→        y_train = train_df[\"target\"]\n   237→        X_valid = valid_df[self.feature_names]\n   238→        y_valid = valid_df[\"target\"]\n   239→\n   240→        # Evolve a fresh population on the training set\n   241→        pop = Population(\n   242→            population_size=ModelConfig.POPULATION_SIZE,\n   243→            model_types=ModelConfig.MODEL_TYPES,\n   244→            mutation_rate=ModelConfig.MUTATION_RATE,\n   245→            crossover_rate=ModelConfig.CROSSOVER_RATE,\n   246→            elitism_count=ModelConfig.ELITISM_COUNT\n   247→        )\n   248→        pop.initialize(input_dim=X_train.shape[1], feature_names=self.feature_names)\n   249→\n   250→        for gen in range(ModelConfig.GENERATIONS_PER_ITERATION):\n   251→            print(f\"  Generation {gen+1}/{ModelConfig.GENERATIONS_PER_ITERATION}\", flush=True)\n   252→            # Evaluate individuals on training data\n   253→            for ind in pop.individuals:\n   254→                try:\n   255→                    ind.model.fit(X_train, y_train)\n   256→                    # Use training accuracy as fitness for selection\n   257→                    pred = ind.model.predict(X_train, threshold=0.5)\n   258→                    ind.fitness = (pred == y_train).mean()\n   259→                except Exception as e:\n   260→                    print(f\"    Training error: {e}\", flush=True)\n   261→                    ind.fitness = -1000.0\n   262→\n   263→            # Evolve to next generation, but not after the final generation\n   264→            if gen < ModelConfig.GENERATIONS_PER_ITERATION - 1:\n   265→                print(\"  Evolving to next generation...\", flush=True)\n   266→                pop.evolve()\n   267→                best = pop.get_best(1)[0]\n   268→                print(f\"    Best fitness: {best.fitness:.4f} ({best.model_type})\", flush=True)\n   269→            else:\n   270→                # Final generation: no evolution, just report best\n   271→                best = pop.get_best(1)[0]\n   272→                print(f\"    Final best fitness: {best.fitness:.4f} ({best.model_type})\", flush=True)\n   273→\n   274→        # Prepare close prices for simulation (used later and here)\n   275→        close_prices = valid_df[\"close\"]\n   276→\n   277→        # Re-score individuals on validation set using Sharpe (profitability)\n   278→        print(\"Re-scoring population on validation set (Sharpe-based)...\", flush=True)\n   279→        for i, ind in enumerate(pop.individuals):\n   280→            # Skip individuals that failed training\n   281→            if ind.fitness is None or ind.fitness <= -1000:\n   282→                print(f\"  Skipping individual {i+1}/{len(pop.individuals)} (failed training)\", flush=True)\n   283→                continue\n   284→            try:\n   285→                print(f\"  Rescoring individual {i+1}/{len(pop.individuals)} ({ind.model_type})\", flush=True)\n   286→                # Predict on validation\n   287→                pred_valid = ind.model.predict(X_valid, threshold=0.5)\n   288→                # Ensure pred_valid is a Series with index\n   289→                if isinstance(pred_valid, np.ndarray):\n   290→                    pred_valid = pd.Series(pred_valid, index=X_valid.index)\n   291→                # Create signals series aligned to close_prices (fill missing with -1)\n   292→                signals_ind = pred_valid.reindex(close_prices.index).fillna(-1).astype(int)\n   293→                # Run simulation\n   294→                self.trader.run(signals_ind, close_prices)\n   295→                v_metrics = self.trader.metrics\n   296→                # Use Sharpe as fitness (higher is better)\n   297→                ind.fitness = v_metrics.get('sharpe', -1000)\n   298→                print(f\"    -> Sharpe: {ind.fitness:.4f}\", flush=True)\n   299→                # Preserve validation metrics for later analysis 303→                ind.fitness = -1000.0\n   304→\n   305→        # Get top diverse models based on validation Sharpe\n   306→        top_models = pop.get_diverse_best(n=5)\n   307→\n   308→        # Generate consensus signals on validation set\n   309→        consensus = ConsensusGate(\n   310→            min_models_agree=ConsensusConfig.MIN_MODELS_AGREE,\n   311→            min_confidence=ConsensusConfig.MIN_CONFIDENCE\n   312→        )\n   313→        signals = consensus.decide(top_models, X_valid)\n   314→\n   315→        # Align close prices (indices correspond)\n   316→        close_prices = valid_df[\"close\"]\n   317→\n   318→        # Run simulator on signals\n   319→        self.trader.run(signals, close_prices)\n   320→        metrics = return metrics\n   333→\n   334→    def train_best_models(\n   335→        self,\n   336→        df: pd.DataFrame,\n   337→        population: Population,\n   338→        horizon_data: dict = None\n   339→    ):\n   340→        \"\"\"\n   341→        Train the best models on full recent data and optionally train horizon ensembles.\n   342→        \"\"\"\n   343→        print(\"Training best models 395→        self.top_models = top_models\n   396→\n   397→    def generate_current_signals(\n   398→        self,\n   399→        current_features: pd.DataFrame,\n   400→        use_horizon: bool = Split into recent data for training and current for prediction\n   439→        # Use last 30 days for training, current for signal generation\n   440→        recent_cutoff = df[\"open_time\"].max() - timedelta(days=30)\n   441→        train_df = df[df[\"open_time\"] <= recent_cutoff].copy()\n   442→        current_df = df[df[\"open_time\"] > recent_cutoff].copy()\n   443→\n   444→        # Limit training samples to control memory/time (use most recent samples)\n   445→        if len(train_df) > ModelConfig.MAX_TRAIN_SAMPLES:\n   446→            train_df = train_df.tail(ModelConfig.MAX_TRAIN_SAMPLES).copy()\n   447→            print(f\"Limited training to {len(train_df)} most recent samples\", flush=True)\n   448→\n   449→        if len(train_df) < ValidationConfig.MIN_TRAIN_SAMPLES:\n   450→            print(f\"Insufficient training data: {len(train_df)} samples\", flush=True)\n   451→            return None\n   452→\n   453→        X_train = train_df[self.feature_names]\n   454→        y_train = train_df[\"target\"]\n   455→\n   456→        # 4. Walk-forward validation on historical folds (use recent data to limit folds)\n   460→        if ValidationConfig.MAX_WALK_FORWARD_DAYS is not None:\n   461→            wf_cutoff = df[\"open_time\"].max() - timedelta(days=ValidationConfig.MAX_WALK_FORWARD_DAYS)\n   462→            df_wf = df[df[\"open_time\"] >= wf_cutoff].copy()\n   463→            print(f\"Using {len(df_wf)} recent samples for walk-forward validation (max {ValidationConfig.MAX_WALK_FORWARD_DAYS} days)\", flush=True)\n   464→        else:\n   465→            df_wf = df\n   466→        metrics = self.run_walk_forward(df_wf)\n   467→\n   468→        # 6. Train best models on full recent data and prepare horizon ensemble\n   469→        self.train_best_models(df, population)\n   470→\n   471→        # 7. Generate current signals\n   472→        if len(current_df) > 0:\n   473→            current_features = current_df[self.feature_names]\n   474→            signals = self.generate_current_signals(current_features)\n   475→            print(f\"Generated {len(signals)} current signals\", flush=True)\n   476→            latest_signal = signals.iloc[-1] if len(signals) > 0 else None\n   477→            print(f\"Latest signal: {latest_signal} (1=UP, 0=DOWN, -1=NO TRADE)\", flush=True)\n   478→        else:\n   479→            signals = pd.Series()\n   480→            latest_signal = None\n   481→\n   482→        # 8. Save results\n   483→        self._save_results(metrics, population, signals)\n   484→\n   485→        # Compile full result\n   486→        result = {\n   487→            \"timestamp\": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),\n   488→            \"accuracy\": metrics.get(\"accuracy\", 0.0),\n   489→            \"bets_per_month\": metrics.get(\"bets_per_month\", 0.0),\n   490→            \"sharpe\": metrics.get(\"sharpe\", 0.0),\n   491→            \"max_drawdown\": metrics.get(\"max_drawdown\", 0.0),\n   492→            \"total_return\": metrics.get(\"total_return\", 0.0),\n   493→            \"latest_signal\": int(latest_signal) if latest_signal is not None else None,\n   494→            \"population_fitness\": {str(i): ind.fitness for i, ind in enumerate(population.get_best(5))}\n   495→        }\n   496→\n   497→        print(\"=\" * 60, flush=True)\n   498→        print(\"STEP COMPLETE\", flush=True)\n   499→        print(f\"Metrics: {json.dumps(result, indent=2)}\", flush=True)\n   500→        print(\"=\" * 60, flush=True)\n   501→\n   502→        return result\n   503→\n   504→    def _save_results(self, metrics: dict, population: Population, signals: pd.Series):\n   505→        \"\"\"Save results to disk.\"\"\"\n   506→        timestamp = datetime.utcnow().strftime(\"%Y%m%d_%H%M%S\")\n   507→        run_dir = self.results_dir / timestamp\n   508→        run_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)\n   509→\n   510→        # Save top models\n   518→        top_models = population.get_best(5)\n   519→        model_dir = run_dir / \"models\"\n   520→        model_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)\n   521→        for i, ind in enumerate(top_models):\n   522→            try:\n   523→                ind.model.save(str(model_dir / f\"model_{i}_{ind.model_type}.pkl\"))\n   524→            except Exception as e:\n   525→                print(f\"Could not save model {i}: {e}\", flush=True)\n   526→\n   527→        # Save population metadata\n   528→        pop_data = []\n   529→        for ind in population.individuals[:10]:\n   530→            pop_data.append({\n   531→                \"model_type\": ind.model_type,\n   532→                \"params\": ind.params,\n   533→                \"fitness\": float(ind.fitness)\n   534→            })\n   535→        with open(run_dir / \"population.json\", \"w\") as f:\n   536→            json.dump(pop_data, f, indent=2)\n   537→\n   538→        print(f\"Results saved to {run_dir}\", flush=True)\n   539→\n   540→\n   541→def main():\n   542→    \"\"\"Entry point for running the trading system.\"\"\"\n   543→    print(\"[main] main() started\", flush=True)\n   544→    system = TradingSystem()\n   545→\n   546→    # That means the consensus gate filtered almost all of those 2880 signals to -1 (NO TRADE) because the confidence was below 0.75.\n\nThus the problem is the confidence threshold is too high for these models. Or the models themselves are not calibrated well (predict_proba outputs are low confidence). The data likely has many uncertain points.\n\nGiven the evolution objective, we need to increase signal frequency while maintaining accuracy >=65%. The current accuracy is 1.0 but that's on the (likely small) set of signals that passed consensus. That could be because only the most confident predictions are traded, and those happen to be correct.\n\nSo the next step should: lower the confidence threshold, or lower MIN_MODELS_AGREE to 1, or both. At least MIN_MODELS_AGREE models must agree on direction\n    - Average confidence must exceed MIN_CONFIDENCE\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(\n        self,\n        min_models_agree: int = ConsensusConfig.MIN_MODELS_AGREE,\n        min_confidence: float = ConsensusConfig.MIN_CONFIDENCE\n    ):\n        self.min_models_agree = min_models_agree\n        self.min_confidence = min_confidence\n\n    def decide(\n        self,\n        models: List[Individual],\n        X: pd.DataFrame\n    ) -> pd.Series:\n        \"\"\"\n        Generate final trading signals (UP=1, DOWN=0, NO_TRADE=-1).\n\n        Args:\n            models: list of trained model individuals\n            X: feature DataFrame to predict on\n\n        Returns:\n            Series of signals (1, 0, or -1) aligned to X.index\n        \"\"\"\n        signals = pd.Series(index=X.index, data=0)\n        probas_matrix = []\n\n        for ind in models:\n            try:\n                proba = ind.model.predict_proba(X)\n                probas_matrix.append(proba)\n            except Exception as e:\n                continue\n\n        if not probas_matrix:\n            # No model worked, all NO_TRADE\n            signals[:] = -1\n            return signals\n\n        probas_array = np.array(probas_matrix)  # shape: (n_models, n_samples)\n\n        # Average confidence for each sample\n        avg_proba = probas_array.mean(axis=0)\n\n        # Count models predicting UP\n        up_votes = (probas_array >= 0.5).sum(axis=0)\n\n        down_votes = len(probas_matrix) - up_votes\n\n        # Apply gating rules\n        for i, (avg_p, up, down) in enumerate(zip(avg_proba, up_votes, down_votes)):\n            # Check agreement\n            if up >= self.min_models_agree:\n                direction = 1\n                confidence = avg_p\n            elif down >= self.min_models_agree:\n                direction = 0\n                confidence = 1 - avg_p  # confidence in DOWN is 1 - avg_proba\n            else:\n                signals.iloc[i] = -1\n                continue\n\n            # Check confidence threshold\n            if confidence >= self.min_confidence:\n                signals.iloc[i] = direction\n            else:\n                signals.iloc[i] = -1\n\n        return signals\n\n    def adjust_thresholds(\n        self,\n        recent_performance: Dict[str, float],\n        target_accuracy: float = 0.65,\n        target_bets: float = 90.0\n    ):\n        \"\"\"\n        Dynamically adjust consensus thresholds based on recent performance.\n\n        If accuracy is high but bet count too low: lower min_models_agree or min_confidence\n        If accuracy is low: raise thresholds\n        \"\"\"\n        accuracy = recent_performance.get(\"accuracy\", 0.5)\n        bets_per_month = recent_performance.get(\"bets_per_month\", 0.0)\n\n        if accuracy >= target_accuracy and bets_per_month < target_bets:\n            # Too strict, loosen\n            self.min_models_agree = max(1, self.min_models_agree - 1)\n            self.min_confidence = max(0.5, self.min_confidence - 0.02)\n        elif accuracy < target_accuracy:\n            # Too loose, tighten\n            self.min_models_agree = min(5, self.min_models_agree + 1)\n            self.min_confidence = min(0.8, self.min_confidence + 0.02)\n\n        # Clamp to reasonable ranges\n        self.min_models_agree = max(1, min(5, self.min_models_agree))\n        self.min_confidence = max(0.5, min(0.9, self.min_confidence))\n\n    def get_params(self) -> dict:\n        return {\n            \"min_models_agree\": self.min_models_agree,\n            \"min_confidence\": self.min_confidence\n        }\n","numLines":123,"startLine":1,"totalLines":123}}}
